<div>   
<p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">【摘要】：后疫情时代人类加速从现实世界向虚拟世界迁移，行走于现实与数字之间。元宇宙应运而生成为时代热词，人类迈向了元宇宙时代，步入数字化生存高级形态。当前，人们热议的元宇宙，并非宇宙的一种形态，而是借用了宇宙的隐喻。人们对元宇宙内涵的理解已经超越了文学作品和宇宙理论中的认知。元宇宙建设与发展应该遵循</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">三不</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">原则。元宇宙不能取代现实世界，而是现实世界映射的虚拟数字空间。人类进入元宇宙有三重境界：体验元宇宙、沉浸元宇宙和融入元宇宙。人类进入元宇宙有两种途径：一种是现实人与元宇宙进行沉浸式交互；另一种是人类以数字化身身份融入元宇宙，进行数字社交和数字生存</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月以来，中国对元宇宙研究热度呈现爆发式增长，研究机构争先开展元宇宙研究。元宇宙呈现元宇宙理论、政策法规和标准规范、战略规划与架构设计、关键技术、场景</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">环境构建、应用场景、经济与产业、治理等八大研究趋势。中国、韩国</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">美国等国家率先制定元宇宙政策，推动元宇宙产业发展。元宇宙对变革人类教育具有巨大潜能，在医疗与医学教育中具有广泛的应用前景，与现实世界重塑虚实共融智慧学习环境。尽管元宇宙对变革人类教育具有巨大潜能，但是元宇宙不可能完全取代现实世界中的人类教育。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">【关键词】：后疫情时代；数字化转型；元宇宙；元宇宙孤岛；</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">医学教育；</span>“三不”原则</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">；教育潜能</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 13px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">后疫情时代，全球加快了数字化转型，数字化学习、数字化工作和数字化生活正在成为人们的常态。人类数字素养与技能迅速提升，数字化意识和习惯正在养成。线上虚拟世界成为现实世界的平行世界，人类加速从现实世界向虚拟世界迁移，行走于现实与数字之间</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>5</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">WiFi</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">6<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">人工智能、大数据、物联网、区块链、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">VR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">MR<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">等新一代数字技术发展迅速</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，数字孪生理论技术更加成熟。由此催生了元宇宙，人类迈向了元宇宙时代，步入数字化生存高级形态。其标志是</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年元宇宙成为年度热词和流行语，引发了思想、科技、资本、企业、文化和教育等各界的热议。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙入选国家语言资源监测与研究中心发布的</span>“<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年度十大网络用语”</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、《</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">柯林斯词典</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">》</span>“2021<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年度热词</span>”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、《</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">咬文嚼字</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">》</span>“2021<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年度十大流行语”</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">中国新闻周刊</span>“2021<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年度十大热词</span>”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。此外，北京、上海、江苏、山西、广州、深圳、成都等多地出现元宇宙提案议案，元宇宙成为两会中的热词</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年被誉为元宇宙元年，巨大资本竞相涌入元宇宙，全球掀起了元宇宙浪潮，这必将人类数字文明推向新高度。元宇宙风靡全球，元宇宙作为下一代互联网发展的新形态将开启未来数字世界新时代。元宇宙究竟是什么，将会对人类教育产生哪些影响，未来元宇宙如何变革教育等问题值得深入探讨。</span></p><h1 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; max-width: 100%; font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 21px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1 </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: 黑体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">究竟何为元宇宙</span></h1><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1.1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙的起源</span></h2><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">人类对元宇宙的认识，源自于人类对宇宙的认识。中国古代就有对宇宙的探索，形成了关于宇宙的朴素知识。据词源考证，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“宇宙”一词可以追溯至《庄子·齐物论》中的“奚旁日月</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">挟宇宙</span>”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。战国末期的尸佼说：</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">四方上下曰宇，往古来今曰宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">宇</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">指空间，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">指时间，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">宇宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">体现了</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">时间和空间的统一。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">文学作品中形成对元宇宙认识的萌芽。早在</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1985</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年，何新</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">认为刘再复的散文诗体现了</span>“双元宇宙的象征”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，双元宇宙指两个无限的宇宙，融心灵与存在为一体。心灵是就深邃而言，存在是就广度而言。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1992<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年，</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">美国作家</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">尼尔</span>·<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">斯蒂芬森（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Neal Stephenson</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）在科幻小说《雪崩》（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Snow Crash</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）中提出了</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>metaverse<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">这部小说以</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">21</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">世纪为背景，描绘的元宇宙是一个救援的地方。主角</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Hiro Protagonist</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">带着防护眼镜和耳机进入元宇宙，在数字世界中作为自己定制的化身出现。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从宇宙学看，宇宙的相关概念有母宇宙、婴宇宙、多宇宙、大宇宙、元宇宙、本宇宙、超宇宙等。母宇宙是原始宇宙，可以产生无数个婴宇宙。本宇宙即人类生存的可见宇宙。大宇宙是本宇宙和其它宇宙构成的更大宇宙。本宇宙不是孤立存在的，而是一个多宇宙。元宇宙演化为本宇宙，本宇宙演化为超宇宙。宇宙大爆炸理论认为宇宙起始于奇点，奇点本身就是一种宇宙形态，也就是元宇宙的存在。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">此外，算法领域提出了基于多元宇宙理论的群智能优化算法</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">——</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">多元宇宙优化算法（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Multi-Verse Optimizer,</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">MVO</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。</span></p><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1.</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙的定义和内涵</span></span></h2><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙的概念和内涵引了学界和业界热议，但是尚未形成较为统一的认识。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Metaverse<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">由前缀</span>meta</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（意为元、超越）</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">和词根</span>verse</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">源于</span>universe</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">），直译为元宇宙。当前，人们对元宇宙内涵的理解已经超越了文学作品和宇宙理论中的认知。深刻认识元宇宙及其内涵，需要从宇宙学、哲学、技术、新闻传播、服务、社会、经济、教育和政界等多个语境进行剖析。当前，人们从不同视角对元宇宙的认识主要有以下观点：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从宇宙学视角看，元宇宙是宇宙的初级和低级形态。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">韩民青认为</span>“<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙是比本宇宙层更深入、更广大、更原始的背景宇宙层次或初级宇宙层次</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，具有与本宇宙不同的性质，属于另类宇宙。本宇宙是有元宇宙演化生成的更高一级的宇宙。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">由此可见，元宇宙并不是一个与本宇宙并行的概念。显然，当前人们热议的元宇宙并非宇宙的一种形态，而是借用了宇宙的隐喻。从学理上看，数字宇宙、虚拟宇宙、孪生宇宙等更适合表达当前人们热议的元宇宙。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从哲学视角上看，元宇宙为人类营造了虚拟的数字空间和数字世界，增强了人与动物的本质区别。元宇宙不是客观存在的，而是典型的人造宇宙、人造时空和人造世界。创造和使用元宇宙将成为人类和动物的重要本质区别。元宇宙能够增强人类的思维意识，充分发挥人类的主观能动性，更有利于人类开展现实世界中无法实现的思想实验，为人类探索未来的未知世界提供了新路径。元宇宙将是人类思想的创新实验室，开辟人类创新创造的新时代。未来，人类将进入现实与虚拟相融合的双重宇宙空间，人类需要在双重宇宙空间中转换角色，更需要重构双重社会规范、伦理与道德。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从技术视角看，元宇宙是信息技术的综合集成，描绘了未来的信息技术革命愿景的全景。黄欣荣和曹贤平</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">认为</span>“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙是指人在自然宇宙之外，通过数字技术建构的一个与自然宇宙相映射但又能给人提供自由创造空间的数字虚拟宇宙，并通过对数字宇宙的探索更加充分地认知和利用自然宇宙。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">张夏恒和李想认为</span>“元宇宙是指依托互联网、信息技术、虚拟仿真技术、数字技术等构成的一种沉浸式体验的互联网要素融合形态。”</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从新闻传播角度看，元宇宙正在重新定义新闻，驱动数字新闻业变革，催生了沉浸式新闻。新闻是新近发生的事实的报道，变成了用户对重构的事实的临场感知。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙将推动新闻传播的虚拟互动，以沉浸式叙事的方式创新新闻报道。元宇宙是一个虚拟与现实高度互通，且由闭环经济体构造的开源平台。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">11</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月，韩国首尔发布《元宇宙首尔基本计划</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; word-wrap: break-word !important;">亿韩元</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">打造元宇宙平台，在经济、文化、旅游、教育和民事投诉等政府业务领域建立元宇宙行政服务生态系统。这个基本计划涵盖经济、教育、旅游、通信、城市、行政和基础设施</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">7</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">个领域</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2023</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年将成立虚拟公共服务中心</span>“元宇宙 <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">120 </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">中心”（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Metaverse 120 Center</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，虚拟形象的公职人员将克服时间、空间和语言限制为人们提供公共服务。元宇宙平台将创建虚拟旅游特区，在虚拟空间中复活被摧毁的历史遗迹。此外，首尔还将在元宇宙平台建立首尔金融科技实验室，以构建培育金融科技产业的线上线下集群。在教育领域将创建首尔开放城市大学的虚拟校园，为学习者提供沉浸式学习资源。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从社会视角看，元宇宙是本宇宙的镜像宇宙，可视为人类社会的数字化再现。元宇宙可以突破时间和空间的限制，产生虚拟的人类社会新形态。元宇宙为人类社会的数字化转型提供了新路径，虚拟人是开拓元宇宙的先驱，在虚拟世界构建</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">后人类社会</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">陈刚和董浩宇认为</span>“元宇宙是利用科技手段进行链接与创造的，与现实世界映射与交互的虚拟世界，具备新型社会体系的数字生活空间。”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙必将深刻影响和改变人类的劳动生活、消费生活和精神生活，形成虚拟劳动、虚拟消费和虚拟文化等人类社会生活新方式。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">人类将有两个身份，一个是人类社会的自我，一个是元宇宙社会中的虚拟人。现实世界中的人有生老病死，元宇宙中的虚拟人可以数字永生。在元宇宙社会，数字化社交和数字化生存将成为常态。元宇宙中的虚拟社交对象，既可能是人类的虚拟映射，也可能是智能机器人。当前，元宇宙社会尚处于构建形成的初级阶段，类似于宇宙大爆炸之前的混沌状态，还没有形成虚拟社会秩序和规则。元宇宙社会打破了区域和国界，具有典型的无边界和开放性，呈现出全新的人类数字文明。元宇宙社会治理相对于人类现实社会而言更具有复杂性，未来元宇宙社会治理极具挑战性。以区块链、人工智能等为代表的智能技术是元宇宙社会治理的关键技术，尤其是区块链技术对于构建元宇宙社会的信任机制至关重要。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从经济视角看，元宇宙是数字经济发展的催化剂，元宇宙社会需要构建新兴数字经济体系。互联网对实体经济产生了重大冲击，元宇宙将引发对实体经济的新一轮冲击。数字生产、数字资产、虚拟货币、数字货币、数字交易等成为元宇宙数字经济的构成要素。数字身份为数字资产的创造和消费提供了新经济模式，数字资产与现实资产的双向流通创造新经济体系。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙中的数字资产以非同质化代币（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Non-Fungible Tokens</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">, </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">NFT</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）和</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">非同质化权利（</span>Non-Fungible Rights<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">NFR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）的形态存在，并引发虚拟商业模式变革和数字经济生产、流通和消费模式的重构。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从教育角度看，元宇宙是在线教育发展的新形态，开启虚拟现实教育新图景</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2003<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年，美国林登实验室</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">创建的虚拟世界</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Second Life</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">是具有代表性的元宇宙形态。在</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Second Life</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">教育功能模块中，能够购买教育用地、创建虚拟学校、开设虚拟课堂和虚拟讲座、进入虚拟图书馆、开展教学实验和技能训练等。在教育领域涌现了教育元宇宙和学习元宇宙的理念。刘革平、高楠</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">等认为</span>“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">教育元宇宙是利用</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">VR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">MR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、数字孪生、</span>5</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">人工智能、区块链等新兴信息技术塑造的虚实融合教育环境，是虚拟与现实全面交织、人类与机器全面联结、学校与社会全面互动的智慧教育环境高阶形态。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">华子荀和付道明认为</span>“学习元宇宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Metaverse for Learning</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">是在元宇宙技术基础上构建起来的学习场景，</span> <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">融合了现实学习空间与虚拟学习空间，并通过数字孪生、区块链技术等实现虚实空间的相互映射与动态交互。</span>”</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从政界来看，元宇宙引发了政界的高度关注，政府积极响应元宇宙可能带给人类的机遇与挑战，迅速超前部署元宇宙发展战略</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">11</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月，俄罗斯卫星网报道，巴巴多斯将成为首个在</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">中设立大使馆的主权国家，在虚拟世界平台中推动与各国政府的双边关系</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">12</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月，管筱璞和李云舒在中央纪委国家监委网站发文《元宇宙如何改写人类社会生活》，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">畅想了元宇宙将会对人类社会生活带来的变化，同时提出需要理性看待元宇宙带来的新一轮科技革命对社会的影响。上海、浙江、海南等在技术、产业等战略规划中，超前部署元宇宙技术研发和产业发展</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2022</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年，上海徐汇区首次将元宇宙写入政府工作报告，将探索成立元宇宙创新联盟。武汉、合肥、成都等政府工作报告都提及元宇宙。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">通过以上对元宇宙认识的分析，可以得出以下基本观点：第一，当前人们热议的元宇宙不是宇宙学视角的元宇宙，也不是宇宙学的一种形态，而是借用的了宇宙的隐喻表达虚拟的数字世界。确切来说，数字宇宙、虚拟宇宙、孪生宇宙等是一种更贴切的表达方式。第二，元宇宙既是数字化理念，又是数字技术的集成，还是数字空间和数字世界。第三，元宇宙是典型的人造物，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">不仅需要</span>VR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">MR</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、触觉互联网、人工智能、区块链、仿真技术等关键技术支撑，更需要元宇宙相关理论、方法、解决方案、标准等方面的创新与突破。第四，正如虫洞是连结两个遥远时空的空间隧道，移动互联网</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>5</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">WiFi</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">6<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">卫星互联网和触觉互联网（技能互联网）是人类穿越现实世界和元宇宙的通道。第五，元宇宙将会对人类社会发展产生重大影响，元宇宙对变革人类社会具有巨大潜能，人们对元宇宙的未来发展充满了殷切的期待。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙建设与发展应该遵循</span>“三不”原则</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">“<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">不能脱离</span>”“<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">不能取代</span>”“<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">不能挑战</span>”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; caret-color: rgb(51, 51, 51); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 20.399999618530273px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">第一条</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">原则：元宇宙不能脱离现实世界而孤立存在，元宇宙是现实世界的映射或镜像，当然也有可能突破现实世界的时间和空间限制而在一定程度上超越现实世界。元宇宙不像现实世界一样具有实体，而是现实世界实体的虚拟化身，或是人类构造的虚拟体。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; caret-color: rgb(51, 51, 51); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 20.399999618530273px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">第二条</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">原则：元宇宙不能取代现实世界，而是与现实世界深度融合，人类数字生存或虚拟生存不能取代现实生存。元宇宙是现实世界的补充和拓展，而非替代关系。元宇宙延伸人类生活空间，拓展人类感知能力，丰富人类生存体验。人类全部沉浸于数字生存，也就失去了生存的价值和意义。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; caret-color: rgb(51, 51, 51); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 17px; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 20.399999618530273px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">第三条</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">原则：元宇宙不能挑战人类三大底线：法律底线、道德底线和人伦底线。现实世界的人生观、价值观和世界观，在元宇宙仍有其价值。元宇宙中的虚拟人需要遵守现实世界所构建的法律、道德和伦理，维护元宇宙和平，促进虚拟人共同发展。</span></p><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1.3</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙的本质与特征</span></h2><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">人们从技术、功能等视角分析了元宇宙的本质。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Li</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Jun<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">认为“元宇宙的本质是将现实世界与通过虚拟现实技术映射的概念或虚拟世界结合起来</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">亚马逊云科技</span>re:Invent<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">全球大会上认为“元宇宙的本质是云计算”</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2022<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月，首尔国立大学医学院的教授发起了“医学元宇宙研究协会”，协会领导者</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Park Chul-kee</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">认为“元宇宙的本质是相聚（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">togetherness</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。如果有可能与他人分享和体验特定的三维空间和时间，无论是在现实中还是在虚拟现实中，这就是元宇宙。”</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">聂辉华和李靖认为</span>“元宇宙的本质在于互联互通</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>interconnectivity<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，否则只是一个个孤立的游戏平台或者社交平台。</span>”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从不同的视角看，元宇宙本质有多样化表达。宇宙学视角中的元宇宙本质是一种宇宙形态。从时空观看，元宇宙本质是平行于现实宇宙的数字宇宙。元宇宙与虚拟现实和增强现实有一定的区别，并不一定完全依赖于虚拟现实或增强现实环境，元宇宙可以在多样化的平台和终端访问。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">关于元宇宙的特征主要有下列观点</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">：</span>Roblox<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">的创始人 </span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">David Baszucki</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">提出元宇宙有八个关键特征：身份（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Identity</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、朋友（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Friends</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、沉浸感（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Immersion</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、低延迟（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">lLow latency</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、多样性（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Diversification</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、随时随地（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Anytime</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">陈刚和董浩宇界定了元宇宙的五大特征与属性</span><span style="margin: 0px;
