box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">Trade & Transaction</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。</span>Jagreet Kaur Gill</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">认为元宇宙有五大特征：持久性</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Persistence<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">同步性</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Synchronicity<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">可用性</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Availability<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">和互操作性</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Interoperability<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">还有学者提出元宇宙有五大特征：社交性</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Sociality<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">没有硬件限制</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>No hardware limitations<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">用户生成内容</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>User-generated content:<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">生存与呼吸</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Living and breathing<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">连接世界</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>Bridged worlds<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从元宇宙特征看，当前人们在线学习、在线办公、在线会议等不能称为元宇宙，只能看作是元宇宙的萌芽状态。数字映射的虚拟人（虚拟身份）、沉浸感、数字社交、数字经济、智能互联、在线触觉交互、在线技能交互、数字创造等八大特征是人类进入元宇宙的重要标志。</span></p><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1.4</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙与现实世界的关系</span></h2><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙与现实世界的关系见图</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙不能取代现实世界，而是现实世界映射的虚拟数字空间。元宇宙不能脱离现实世界而孤立存在，元宇宙与现实世界都是本宇宙的一部分。人类呈现三种形态：现实人、半数人、虚拟人</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">数字人（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AI<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">虚拟主播</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）。在现实世界中，人类以现实形态存在；在元宇宙中，人类以半数人和虚拟人</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">数字人（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AI<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">虚拟主播</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）的形态存在。机器人在现实世界中以实体机器人形态存在，机器人在元宇宙以虚拟机器人形态存在。人类与机器人在现实世界和元宇宙中以人机共生、人机共融、人机共创的方式存在。在现实世界中身份证</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">护照是人类的身份标识，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">在元宇宙中</span>NFT<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">是人类的数字身份标识</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。人类进入元宇宙有三重境界：体验元宇宙、沉浸元宇宙和融入元宇宙。人类进入元宇宙有两种途径：一种是现实人通过全息投影、触觉手套、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">VR<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">头显等与元宇宙进行沉浸式交互</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">；另一种是人类以半数人、虚拟人</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">数字人（</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AI<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">虚拟主播</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）的数字化身身份融入元宇宙，进行数字社交和数字生存。在元宇宙中，数字身份、数字永生、数字生存、数字社交、数字孪生、数字资产等都是现实世界的数字映射。人类通过移动互联网</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">（</span>5</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">/6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">G</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">WiFi</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">6<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）、</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">卫星互联网和触觉互联网（技能互联网）畅游于现实世界和元宇宙之间，在虚实之中实现虚实共生和虚实共创，构筑人类数字文明新生态。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: center; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span></p><p style="white-space: normal; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙研究与发展现状</span></span></h1><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">从全球看，中国、韩国等国家学者率先开展了元宇宙相关研究</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span>2021</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">月以来，全球关于元宇宙的研究热度持续增加，逐渐涌现了元宇宙相关的学术论文、研究报告、白皮书、新闻报道等。据百度指数统计</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">年</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">等。总体来说，元宇宙研究呈现爆炸式增加，引发了研究者的高度关注。元宇宙研究可以归纳为两大类：一类是从宇宙学角度研究元宇宙；另一类是借助元宇宙隐喻，从计算机、教育学、医学、经济等其他学科视角研究元宇宙。人们对元宇宙的态度可以分为三种：一是积极拥抱元宇宙，体现了技术乐观主义；</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">二是认为元宇宙是</span>“伪概念”“伪命题”“资本骗局”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，存在重大风险隐患等，体现了技术悲观主义；三是对元宇宙持观望态度，理性看待元宇宙将会对人类和社会发展产生的影响与变革，体现了技术中性论。</span></p><h2 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 21px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 25.600000381469727px; font-family: Calibri; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2.</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙八大研究趋势</span></h2><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">调研国内外研究文献，结合元宇宙产业发展情况，梳理发现元宇宙呈现八大研究趋势：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">一是元宇宙理论。元宇宙还是新鲜事物，未来需要加强元宇宙定义、内涵、本质、特征等方面的研究。元宇宙理论基础有沉浸理论、虚拟现实理论、增强现实理论、不完全契约理论、开放复杂巨系统理论、大成智慧学、复杂性科学、媒介规范理论、三个世界理论（物理世界、精神世界、知识世界）等。元宇宙是复杂的人造系统，需要从哲学、社会学、管理学、教育学、人工智能等多学科和跨学科角度开展研究。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">二元宇宙政策法规和标准规范。元宇宙已经吸引了政界关注，地方政府率先发布了元宇宙政策，致力于抢占新一轮科技革命。元宇宙中的虚拟人行为犯罪，与之对应的现实人需要承担法律责任。元宇宙中的行为主体，需要遵循元宇宙虚拟社会规范和伦理道德。现实世界的政策法规是否适合虚拟世界，如何构建适切元宇宙的政策法规，元宇宙将会对现实政策法规产生哪些冲击和影响，以及元宇宙标准规范等都亟待研究。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">三是元宇宙战略规划与架构设计。当前，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙产品还是</span>“元宇宙孤岛”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，多个元宇宙产品之间实现智能互联是一项重大的挑战。元宇宙智能互联也是提升人类宇宙感的重要战略。元宇宙是典型的复杂人造宇宙，由此决定了战略规划与架构设计的重要性。元宇宙体系架构包括体系参考模型、系统互操作、应用行为逻辑、技术参考架构、分层核心技术等。未来继续加强元宇宙战略规划与架构设计研究，迫切需要开展多领域的元宇宙架构设计研究。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">四是元宇宙关键技术。元宇宙是数字技术的集成，涉及五类技术</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">：（</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">新型通信技术，如</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">移动互联网（</span>5G/6G<span style="margin: 0px; font-family: "Times New Roman"; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">WiFi6</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">加快了人类迈向</span>“人机共融”“人机共创”时代</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。（</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">）</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">已经成为人类学习解剖知识的重要资源</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">、焦虑症治疗、抑郁症治疗、物理治疗、心理治疗等方面具有广泛的应用。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AR<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">可以帮助外科医生进行精准操作提高手术效率</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，例如，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">利用</span>AR<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">手术导航技术</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，可以让医生事先了解患者身体结构，更加精准的开展脊柱、心外、开颅、器官移植等复杂手术。</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">AR<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">技术可以清晰展示患者体内静脉位置</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，让护士更容易尽心静脉注射。传统的医学影像诊断需要依靠人工识别，人工智能辅助诊断可以显著提高诊断的精准率，降低影像医生工作量。由此，改变外科医生的学习方式，突破用塑料模型或遗体进行教学的方式，而且可以重复开展多种外科手术技能训练，加快培养专家型医生。人工智能在医疗影像诊断领域具有极大潜能和广阔的应用前景。基于</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">5</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">二是元宇宙具有较强的</span>“沉浸感”“真实感”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">，可以更有效地开展基于虚实触觉交互、情感交互、感知交互的沉浸学习、实景学习和仿真学习。三是元宇宙通过数字孪生连接现实教育系统，有助于开展教育系统发展的仿真推演与仿真治理，为现实世界教育治理提供决策依据。四是元宇宙营造跨越现实世界的虚拟时空，突破现实世界的时空限制，人们可以在元宇宙中畅游思想之旅，开展元宇宙实验，验证现实世界中的思想实验。五是元宇宙赋予人类数字永生，拓展人类生存场域，有助于人类突破物理现实、拓展生命体验，激发人类创新欲望，释放人类创造力。</span></p><h1 style="white-space: normal; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; font-size: 14px; max-width: 100%; font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; break-after: avoid; line-height: 21px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> 4</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 黑体; font-weight: normal; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">元宇宙未来教育应用展望</span></span></h1><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">当前，人们对元宇宙寄予厚望，殷切期待元宇宙给人类社会带来的深刻影响和变革。元宇宙作为典型的智能人造物，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">符合机器人的</span>“恐怖谷理论”</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; font-family: 宋体; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;">。当元宇宙和现实世界相似达到特定的程度，人们则会容易混淆现实世界和元宇宙，对元宇宙表现出反感和抵制。元宇宙不能取代现实世界，而是与现实世界共生、共融、共创。尽管元宇宙变革人类教育具有巨大潜能，但是元宇宙不可能完全取代现实世界中的人类教育。元宇宙不能改变人类教育的本质，而是丰富了人类学习资源形态，延伸了人类学习活动，拓展了人类学习和教学方式，重塑了一种虚拟智慧学习环境，形成了虚实共融教育系统新生态。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 16.799999237060547px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 宋体; line-height: 19.200000762939453px; font-size: 16px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"> </span></p><p style="white-space: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; padding: 0px; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; letter-spacing: 0.5440000295639038px; text-align: justify; font-family: Calibri; font-size: 14px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;"><br></p><p>详见：</p><p>[1]王运武,王永忠,王藤藤,姜松雪,李雪婷.元宇宙的起源、发展及教育意蕴[J].中国医学教育技术:1-9[2022-02-25].</p><p><br></p>                    <br><br>
